Private Sub ApNewYearEveningButton_Click()

Sheet1.Shapes("Rectangle 10").Visible = msoTrue
Call April_New_Year_Evening

End Sub

Private Sub CheckBox0130AM1_Click()

If Sheet1.CheckBox0130AM1.Value = True Then

    'Do Nothing

Else

    Dim CheckName As String
    CheckName = Sheet2.Range("B7").Text

    Sheet23.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet23.Range("D7:S7").ClearContents          'Curfew
    Sheet23.Range("Z7:AO7").ClearContents         'Weekdays
    Sheet23.Range("AU7:BJ7").ClearContents        'Saturday
    Sheet23.Range("BP7:CE7").ClearContents        'Sunday
    Sheet23.Range("CK7:CZ7").ClearContents        'April New Year
    
    MsgBox " " & CheckName & " 1.30PM Delivery Data Successfully Cleared", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "Production Programme"
    
    Sheet23.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
    Call Re_Call_6_00AM_Production
    
    Sheet1.CheckBox0130AM1.Enabled = False

End If

End Sub

Private Sub ExtraProductionCheckBox_Click()

If Sheet1.ExtraProductionCheckBox.Value = True Then

    '*********************

Else

    MsgBox "Every Month 25 to 07 Extra Production Successfully Stoped", vbExclamation + vbOKOnly, "                                 *** Extra Production Calculation ***"
    
    Sheet1.ExtraProductionCheckBox.Visible = False
    
    If Sheet23.Range("U1").Value = "Extra Enabled" Then
    
        Application.Quit
        Application.ActiveWindow.Close SaveChanges:=False
        ThisWorkbook.Close SaveChanges:=False
    
    End If

End If

End Sub

Private Sub MorningApNewYearButton_Click()

Sheet1.SummaryPrint5AMButton.Visible = True

Sheet1.MorningPoyaButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningCurfewButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningSaturdayButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningWeekdaysButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningSundayButton.Enabled = False

Sheet1.TextBoxProductionActivated.Value = "Activated"

'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data

    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("DG7:DU76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Range("B3").Value = "April New Year"
    
    Sheet2.Range("C1").Value = "5.00 am Production April New Year.xlsm"
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
    Sheet1.Range("D5").Select
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Rounded Rectangular Callout 1").Visible = msoTrue
    
    MsgBox "April New Year 5.00AM Production Plan Ready to Launch", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "Production Programme"
    
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("0:00:03"))
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Rounded Rectangular Callout 1").Visible = msoFalse

    If Sheet2.Range("D77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("E77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox0.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox0.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox0.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("F77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox1.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox1.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox1.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("G77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox2.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox2.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox2.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("H77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox3.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox3.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox3.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("I77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox4.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox4.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox4.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("J77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox5.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox5.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox5.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("K77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox6.Enabled = False
    
    Else
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox6.Value = True
        Sheet1.CheckBox6.Enabled = True
        
    End If
    
    If Sheet2.Range("L77").Value <= 0 Then
    
        Sheet1.CheckBox7.Enabled = False
    
    Else

Private Sub PlainRollGenerateButton_Click()

Dim FiveAMPlan As String
FiveAMPlan = Sheet1.Range("R2").Text

Dim SixAMPlan As String
SixAMPlan = Sheet1.Range("R3").Text

Dim Weekdays As String
Weekdays = "Weekdays"

Dim Saturday As String
Saturday = "Saturday"

Dim Sunday As String
Sunday = "Sunday"

'Sheet2 (Delivery Summary)
Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

'Sheet23 (10.30 & 2.30 Delivery Summary)
Sheet23.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

'Sheet24 (5.00AM Delivery Summary)
Sheet24.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

If FiveAMPlan = Weekdays Then

    Sheet2.Select
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").Select

    'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data
    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("AP7:AP76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
ElseIf FiveAMPlan = Saturday Then

    Sheet2.Select
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").Select

    'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data
    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("BK7:BK76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
    
ElseIf FiveAMPlan = Sunday Then

    Sheet2.Select
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").Select

    'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data
    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("CF7:CF76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("F7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
End If


If SixAMPlan = Weekdays Then

    Sheet2.Select
    
    Sheet2.Range("G7").Select

    'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data
    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet23.Range("AP164:AP233").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("G7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
ElseIf SixAMPlan = Saturday Then

    Sheet2.Select
    
    Sheet2.Range("G7").Select

    'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data
    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet23.Range("BK164:BK233").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("G7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
ElseIf SixAMPlan = Sunday Then

    Sheet2.Select

    Sheet23.Range("CF164:CF233").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("G7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

End If

'Sheet2 (Delivery Summary)
Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

'Sheet23 (10.30 & 2.30 Delivery Summary)
Sheet23.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

'Sheet24 (5.00AM Delivery Summary)
Sheet24.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

Sheet1.Select

    Sheet6.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
    Sheet6.PageSetup.Orientation = xlPortrait
    Sheet6.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
    Sheet6.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
    Sheet6.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$B$378:$I$423"
    Sheet6.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
            
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("0:00:03"))
            
    Sheet6.PrintOut
    
    Sheet21.Select
    
    MsgBox "                *** Successfully Printed ***" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & "This Programme is Automatically Shutting Down" _
        , vbOKOnly + vbInformation, "*** Powered by Viraj Lakshan Rathnayake ***"
    
        Application.Quit
        Application.ActiveWindow.Close SaveChanges:=False
        ThisWorkbook.Close SaveChanges:=False

End Sub

Private Sub SummaryPrint5AMButton_Click()

Dim FiveAMProd As String
FiveAMProd = "5.00AM Delivery Production Programme"

Dim CurrySheet As String
CurrySheet = "Curry Sheet Programme"

Dim CheckApplication As String
CheckApplication = Sheet21.Range("B4").Text

Dim CheckDeliverySummaryValue As String
CheckDeliverySummaryValue = Sheet2.Range("X77").Value

If CheckApplication = FiveAMProd Then

    If CheckDeliverySummaryValue = 0 Then
    
        MsgBox "*** Invalid Authontication ***", vbCritical + vbOKOnly, "Production Programme"
        
    Else

        'Sheet2 (Delivery Summary)
        Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
        Sheet2.Range("A1").AutoFilter Field:=1, Criteria1:="Y"
    
        Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
        Sheet2.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4  'A3
        Sheet2.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape  'Potrait
        Sheet2.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
        Sheet2.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
        Sheet2.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$B$2:$W$76"
        Sheet2.PrintOut Copies:=1
    
        Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
        MsgBox "*** Successfully Printed ***", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "Production Programme"
        
    End If

ElseIf CheckApplication = CurrySheet Then

        'Print 10.30AM & 1.30PM Delivery Summary
        Sheet23.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

        Dim ProductionPlanName As String
        ProductionPlanName = Sheet2.Range("B3").Value
        
        If ProductionPlanName = "Weekdays" Then
        
                Sheet23.Range("A1:AQ155").AutoFilter Field:=23, Criteria1:="Y"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
                Sheet23.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$X$2:$AP$77, $X$80:$AP$155"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
                
                Sheet23.PrintOut Copies:=2
    
                Sheet23.ShowAllData
            
        ElseIf ProductionPlanName = "Saturday" Then
        
                Sheet23.Range("A1:AR155").AutoFilter Field:=44, Criteria1:="Y"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
                Sheet23.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$AS$2:$BK$77, $AS$80:$BK$155"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
                
                Sheet23.PrintOut Copies:=2
    
                Sheet23.ShowAllData
        
        
        ElseIf ProductionPlanName = "Sunday" Then
        
                Sheet23.Range("A1:BM155").AutoFilter Field:=65, Criteria1:="Y"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
                Sheet23.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$BN$2:$CF$77, $BN$80:$CF$155"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
                
                Sheet23.PrintOut Copies:=2
    
                Sheet23.ShowAllData
            
        ElseIf ProductionPlanName = "Curfew" Then
        
                Sheet23.Range("A1:A155").AutoFilter Field:=1, Criteria1:="Y"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
                Sheet23.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$B$2:$T$77, $B$80:$T$155"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
                
                Sheet23.PrintOut Copies:=2
    
                Sheet23.ShowAllData
            
        ElseIf ProductionPlanName = "April New Year" Then
        
                Sheet23.Range("A1:CH155").AutoFilter Field:=86, Criteria1:="Y"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.PaperSize = xlPaperA4
                Sheet23.PageSetup.Orientation = xlLandscape
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesTall = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.FitToPagesWide = 1
                Sheet23.PageSetup.PrintArea = "$CI$2:$DA$77, $CI$80:$DA$155"

                Sheet23.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"

                Sheet23.ShowAllData

        Sheet23.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

End If

End Sub

Private Sub Worksheet_Activate()

Sheet1.DisplayPageBreaks = False

Dim FiveAMProd As String
FiveAMProd = "5.00AM Delivery Production Programme"

Dim CurrySheet As String
CurrySheet = "Curry Sheet Programme"

Dim Anytime_Recipe_Generator As String
Anytime_Recipe_Generator = "Anytime Recipe Generator"

Dim CheckApplication As String
CheckApplication = Sheet21.Range("B4").Text

Dim Username As String, Rng As Range
Username = Sheet21.Range("U1").Text

Set Rng = Worksheets("Users").Range("B2:F7")

Dim UsernameCheck As String

On Error Resume Next
UsernameCheck = Application.WorksheetFunction.VLookup(Username, Rng, 1, False)
On Error GoTo 0

If UsernameCheck = "Viraj" Or UsernameCheck = "Dulan" Then
    
    
    
Else

    If CheckApplication = Anytime_Recipe_Generator Then
    
        'Do Not Run
    
    Else

        Dim Sunday As String
        Sunday = Sheet2.Range("B1").Text

        If Sunday = "Sunday" Then

            Call Sunday_Notification

        End If
        
    End If
    
End If


    
End Sub

'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data

    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("CL7:CZ76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary

Private Sub MorningSaturdayButton_Click()

Sheet1.SummaryPrint5AMButton.Visible = True

Sheet1.MorningPoyaButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningCurfewButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningSundayButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningWeekdaysButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningApNewYearButton.Enabled = False

Sheet1.TextBoxProductionActivated.Value = "Activated"

'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data

    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("AV7:BJ76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Range("B3").Value = "Saturday"
    
    Sheet2.Range("C1").Value = "5.00 am Production Saturday.xlsm"
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
    Sheet1.Range("D5").Select
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Rounded Rectangular Callout 1").Visible = msoTrue
    
    MsgBox "Saturday 5.00AM Production Plan Ready to Launch", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "Production Programme"

    Sheet1.Shapes("Rounded Rectangular Callout 1").Visible = msoFalse

Private Sub MorningSundayButton_Click()

Sheet1.SummaryPrint5AMButton.Visible = True

Sheet1.MorningPoyaButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningCurfewButton.Enabled = False

Sheet1.MorningApNewYearButton.Enabled = False

'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data

    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("BQ7:CE76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Range("B3").Value = "Sunday"

Private Sub MorningWeekdaysButton_Click()

Sheet1.SummaryPrint5AMButton.Visible = True

Sheet1.MorningPoyaButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningSaturdayButton.Enabled = False
Sheet1.MorningSundayButton.Enabled = False

Sheet1.MorningApNewYearButton.Enabled = False

'Copy & Paste 5.00AM Delivery Data

    Sheet2.Unprotect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"

    Sheet24.Range("AA7:AO76").Copy '5.00AM 3X Delivery
    
    Sheet2.Range("E7").PasteSpecial xlPasteValues 'Delivery Summary
    
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    Sheet2.Range("B3").Value = "Weekdays"
    
    Sheet2.Range("C1").Value = "5.00 am Production Weekdays.xlsm"
    
    Sheet2.Protect Password:="Admin@donandsons.lk54321"
    
    Sheet1.Range("D5").Select
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Rounded Rectangular Callout 1").Visible = msoTrue

If CheckBox.Value = False Then

Sheet2.Range("D7:D76").ClearContents    'Delivery Summary

'*********************************** Curfew ***********************************
Sheet23.Range("D7:D76").ClearContents   '(10.30AM & 1.30PM Summary) - 1.30PM
Sheet23.Range("D85:D154").ClearContents '(10.30AM & 1.30PM Summary) - 10.30AM
'******************************************************************************

Private Sub MainProductionButton_Click()

Dim ActivatedStatus As String
ActivatedStatus = "Activated"

If Sheet1.TextBoxProductionActivated = ActivatedStatus Then

    '***********************************************************************************************************
    '********************************************* Saturday 5.00AM *********************************************
    '***********************************************************************************************************

    Dim ThisWorkbookName As String
    ThisWorkbookName = Sheet2.Range("C1").Text

    Dim SaturdayWorkbook As String
    SaturdayWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Saturday.xlsm"

    Dim SundayWorkbook As String
    SundayWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Sunday.xlsm"

    Dim WeekdaysWorkbook As String
    WeekdaysWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Weekdays.xlsm"

    Dim PoyaWorkbook As String
    PoyaWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Poya.xlsm"

    Dim CurfewWorkbook As String
    CurfewWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Curfew.xlsm"
    
    Dim AprilNewYearWorkbook As String
    AprilNewYearWorkbook = "5.00 am Production April New Year.xlsm"

    Dim TomarrowDay As String
    TomarrowDay = Sheet2.Range("B1").Text

    If ThisWorkbookName = SaturdayWorkbook Then

       Dim Saturday As String
      Saturday = "Saturday"

        If TomarrowDay = Saturday Then

            Call Production_Plan
        
        Else
    
            Call Saturday_5AM
            
        End If

    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = SundayWorkbook Then

        Dim Sunday As String
        Sunday = "Sunday"

        If TomarrowDay = Sunday Then
    
            Call Production_Plan
        
        Else

            Call Sunday_5AM
        
        End If
    
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = WeekdaysWorkbook Then

        Dim Weekday1 As String
        Weekday1 = "Monday"

        Dim Weekday2 As String
        Weekday2 = "Tuesday"

        Dim Weekday3 As String
        Weekday3 = "Wednesday"

        Dim Weekday4 As String
        Weekday4 = "Thursday"

        Dim Weekday5 As String
        Weekday5 = "Friday"

        If TomarrowDay = Weekday1 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday2 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday3 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday4 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday5 Then
    
            Call Production_Plan
        
        Else
    
            Call Weekdays_5AM
        
        End If
    
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = PoyaWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(255, 192, 0)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "Tomorrow is Poya Day"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Production_Plan
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
     
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = CurfewWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(255, 102, 0)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "You Selected to Curfew?"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Production_Plan
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
        
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = AprilNewYearWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(0, 255, 255)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "You Selected to April New Year?"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Production_Plan
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
    
    Else

    MsgBox "This Workbook Name is Not Matched to Programmed Names" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "                 Please Contact System Administrator      ", vbOKOnly + vbCritical, _
           "                           *** Powered by Viraj Lakshan Rathnayake ***"

    End If
    
Else

    Sheet1.Range("D5").Select

    Sheet1.Shapes("Speech Bubble: Rectangle with Corners Rounded 9").Visible = msoTrue

    MsgBox "     Please Select The Production Detail First" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "                               Or                  " & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "     Please Contact System Administrator      ", vbOKOnly + vbCritical, _
           "               *** Powered by Viraj Lakshan Rathnayake ***"
           
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Speech Bubble: Rectangle with Corners Rounded 9").Visible = msoFalse

End If

End Sub

Private Sub ShorteatsSectionButton_Click()

Dim ActivatedStatus As String
ActivatedStatus = "Activated"

If Sheet1.TextBoxProductionActivated = ActivatedStatus Then

    '************************************************************************************************************
    '********************************************* Shorteats 5.00AM *********************************************
    '************************************************************************************************************

    Dim ThisWorkbookName As String
    ThisWorkbookName = Sheet2.Range("C1").Text

    Dim SaturdayWorkbook As String
    SaturdayWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Saturday.xlsm"

    Dim SundayWorkbook As String
    SundayWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Sunday.xlsm"

    Dim WeekdaysWorkbook As String
    WeekdaysWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Weekdays.xlsm"

    Dim PoyaWorkbook As String
    PoyaWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Poya.xlsm"

    Dim CurfewWorkbook As String
    CurfewWorkbook = "5.00 am Production Curfew.xlsm"
    
    Dim AprilNewYearWorkbook As String
    AprilNewYearWorkbook = "5.00 am Production April New Year.xlsm"

    Dim TomarrowDay As String
    TomarrowDay = Sheet2.Range("B1").Text
    
    If ThisWorkbookName = SaturdayWorkbook Then

        Dim Saturday As String
        Saturday = "Saturday"

        If TomarrowDay = Saturday Then
    
            Call Shorteats_Curry
    
        Else
    
            Call Saturday_11_30AM
        
        End If
    
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = SundayWorkbook Then

        Dim Sunday As String
        Sunday = "Sunday"

        If TomarrowDay = Sunday Then

            Call Shorteats_Curry
        
        Else
        
            Call Sunday_11_30AM
        
        End If

    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = WeekdaysWorkbook Then

        Dim Weekday1 As String
        Weekday1 = "Monday"

        Dim Weekday2 As String
        Weekday2 = "Tuesday"

        Dim Weekday3 As String
        Weekday3 = "Wednesday"

        Dim Weekday4 As String
        Weekday4 = "Thursday"

        Dim Weekday5 As String
        Weekday5 = "Friday"

        If TomarrowDay = Weekday1 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday2 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday3 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday4 Or TomarrowDay = Weekday5 Then

            Call Shorteats_Curry
        
        Else
    
            Call Weekday_11_30AM
        
        End If
    
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = PoyaWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(255, 192, 0)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "Tomorrow is Poya Day"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Shorteats_Curry
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
     
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = CurfewWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(255, 102, 0)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "You Selected to Curfew?"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Shorteats_Curry
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
        
    ElseIf ThisWorkbookName = AprilNewYearWorkbook Then

        Sheet2.Select
    
        Sheet2.Range("W1").Select

        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(0, 255, 255)
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").TextEffect.Text = "You Selected to April New Year?"
    
        CarryOn = MsgBox("Do You Want to Generate???", vbInformation + vbYesNo, "*** 5.00AM Production Programme ***")
    
        Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
        Sheet2.Shapes("Oval Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse
    
        If CarryOn = vbYes Then
     
            Call Shorteats_Curry
     
        ElseIf CarryOn = vbNo Then
     
            'Back To Order
            Sheet1.Select
     
        End If
    
    Else

    MsgBox "This Workbook Name is Not Matched to Programmed Names" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "                 Please Contact System Administrator      ", vbOKOnly + vbCritical, _
           "                           *** Powered by Viraj Lakshan Rathnayake ***"

    End If

Else

    Sheet1.Range("D5").Select

    Sheet1.Shapes("Rectangular Callout 3").Visible = msoTrue

    MsgBox "     Please Select The Production Detail First" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "                               Or                  " & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
           "     Please Contact System Administrator      ", vbOKOnly + vbCritical, _
           "               *** Powered by Viraj Lakshan Rathnayake ***"
           
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("00:00:03"))
    
    Sheet1.Shapes("Rectangular Callout 3").Visible = msoFalse

End If

End Sub

If Sheet1.TextBoxProductionActivated = ActivatedStatus Then

        Dim FolderDate As String
        FolderDate = Format(Now() + 1, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    
        Dim sFolderPath As String
    
        sFolderPath = "\\serverml310\desktop\DMS Staff Only (DONT DELETE)\6.00AM Production PDF\" & FolderDate & " - 6.00AM"
    
        If Right(sFolderPath, 1) <> "\" Then
    
            sFolderPath = sFolderPath & "\"
        
        End If
    
        If Dir(sFolderPath, vbDirectory) <> vbNullString Then
    
            'Do Nothing
        
        Else
        
            Dim fdObj As Object
            Application.ScreenUpdating = False
            Set fdObj = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
        
            If fdObj.FolderExists(sFolderPath) Then
        
                'Do Nothing
            
            Else
        
                fdObj.CreateFolder (sFolderPath)
            
            End If
        
            Application.ScreenUpdating = True
        
        End If

Private Sub SpotCurrySheetButton_Click()

Dim CheckProduction As String
CheckProduction = Sheet2.Range("F1").Text

If CheckProduction = "" Then

    Dim CheckAnytimeDate As String
    CheckAnytimeDate = Sheet1.Range("O11").Value
    
    Dim CheckAnytimeTime As String
    CheckAnytimeTime = Sheet1.Range("O12").Value
    
    Dim CheckAnytimeOrder As String
    CheckAnytimeOrder = Sheet1.Range("O13").Value
    
    Dim CheckAnytimeReqNo As String
    CheckAnytimeReqNo = Sheet1.Range("O14").Value
    
    If CheckAnytimeDate = "" Or CheckAnytimeTime = "" Or CheckAnytimeOrder = "" Or CheckAnytimeReqNo = "" Then
    
        MsgBox "Please Enter Anytime Curry Sheet Date, Time & Order", vbCritical + vbOKOnly, "                              *** Production Programme ***"
        
    Else
    
        If CheckAnytimeReqNo = "-" Then
    
            Dim msg As String, Ans As Variant
    
            msg = "Recipe Requestion Number is Not Available" & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & _
                  "         Do You Want To Continue???"
            Ans = MsgBox(msg, vbYesNo + vbCritical, "*** Production Programme ***")

            Select Case Ans

            Case vbYes
            
                Dim wsa As Worksheet
                For Each wsa In Worksheets
                wsa.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
                Next wsa
    
                Sheet4.PageSetup.LeftFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
                Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"

                Sheet4.PageSetup.CenterFooter = ""
            
                Call Anytime_Curry_Sheet_Print
            
            Case vbNo
            
                MsgBox "Please Enter Recipe Requestion Page Number", vbExclamation + vbOKOnly, "*** Production Programme ***"
            
            End Select
            
        Else
        
            Dim wsap As Worksheet
            For Each wsap In Worksheets
            wsap.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
            Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"
            Next wsap
    
            Sheet4.PageSetup.LeftFooter = "&""Cambria,Italic""&B&10This File Was Prepared by " & _
            Environ("username") & " on &D at &T"

            Sheet4.PageSetup.CenterFooter = ""
        
            Call Anytime_Curry_Sheet_Print
            
        End If
        
    End If
    
Else

    Dim CheckActivation As String
    CheckActivation = Sheet2.Range("F1").Text
    
    MsgBox CheckActivation & vbNewLine & vbNewLine & " Please Cloese & Re-open the Programme", vbExclamation + vbOKOnly, "                  Production Programme"

End If
    
End Sub
